### TaskCreate - 2026-02-01 17:12:03 UTC [18:12:03 CEST]

**User Request:** Implement the following plan:

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

## Proposed MkDocs Structure

**Top-level directories in `docs-content/`:**

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `index.md` | Landing page with quick links |
| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |
| `core-systems/` | LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories |
| `architecture/` | System design, health monitoring, data flow |
| `integrations/` | All MCP servers and tools |
| `reference/` | Commands, API, troubleshooting |
| `images/` | Curated images organized by topic |
| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

**Navigation (5 tabs):**
1. **Home** - Quick start, what is coding
2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

---

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation
**Decision: Pull into MkDocs** (user confirmed)
- Consolidate key integration docs into main MkDocs site
- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

---

## Files to Create

**MkDocs config:** `mkdocs.yml`

**Getting Started section:**
- `docs-content/getting-started/index.md`
- `docs-content/getting-started/configuration.md`
- `docs-content/getting-started/docker-mode.md`

**Core Systems section:**

### TaskCreate - 2026-02-01 17:12:03 UTC [18:12:03 CEST]

**User Request:** Implement the following plan:

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

## Proposed MkDocs Structure

**Top-level directories in `docs-content/`:**

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `index.md` | Landing page with quick links |
| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |
| `core-systems/` | LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories |
| `architecture/` | System design, health monitoring, data flow |
| `integrations/` | All MCP servers and tools |
| `reference/` | Commands, API, troubleshooting |
| `images/` | Curated images organized by topic |
| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

**Navigation (5 tabs):**
1. **Home** - Quick start, what is coding
2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

---

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation
**Decision: Pull into MkDocs** (user confirmed)
- Consolidate key integration docs into main MkDocs site
- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

---

## Files to Create

**Getting Started section:**

### TaskCreate - 2026-02-01 17:12:03 UTC [18:12:03 CEST]

**User Request:** Implement the following plan:

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

## Proposed MkDocs Structure

**Top-level directories in `docs-content/`:**

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `index.md` | Landing page with quick links |
| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |
| `core-systems/` | LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories |
| `architecture/` | System design, health monitoring, data flow |
| `integrations/` | All MCP servers and tools |
| `reference/` | Commands, API, troubleshooting |
| `images/` | Curated images organized by topic |
| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

**Navigation (5 tabs):**
1. **Home** - Quick start, what is coding
2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

---

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation
**Decision: Pull into MkDocs** (user confirmed)
- Consolidate key integration docs into main MkDocs site
- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

---

## Files to Create

**MkDocs config:** `mkdocs.yml`

**Getting Started section:**
- `docs-content/getting-started/index.md`
- `docs-content/getting-started/configuration.md`
- `docs-content/getting-started/docker-mode.md`

**Core Systems section:**
- `docs-content/core-systems/index.md`
- `docs-content/core-systems/lsl.md`
- `docs-content/core-systems/ukb-vkb.md`
- `docs-content/core-systems/constraints.md`
- `docs-content/core-systems/trajectories.md`

**Architecture section:**
- `docs-content/architecture/index.md`
- `docs-content/architecture/health-monitoring.md`
- `docs-content/architecture/data-flow.md`

**Integrations section:**
- `docs-content/integrations/index.md`
- `docs-content/integrations/semantic-analysis.md`
- `docs-content/integrations/constraint-monitor.md`
- `docs-content/integrations/browser-access.md`
- `docs-content/integrations/code-graph-rag.md`
- `docs-content/integrations/serena.md`
- `docs-content/integrations/dashboard.md`

**Reference section:**
- `docs-content/reference/index.md`
- `docs-content/reference/commands.md`
- `docs-content/reference/api.md`
- `docs-content/reference/troubleshooting.md`

**Supporting files:**
- `docs-content/stylesheets/extra.css`
- `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`

---

## Key Diagrams to Keep (~30 estimated)

**Architecture:** coding-system-architecture.png, complete-system-overview.png, integration-architecture.png, knowledge-management-architecture.png

**Workflows:** coding-workflow-with-ai.png, knowledge-capture-flow.png, health-verification-flow.png, constraint-violation-handling.png

**Components:** lsl-architecture.png, semantic-analysis-system-overview.png, constraint-monitor-components.png, statusline-architecture.png

**Screenshots:** Health dashboard, VKB visualization

---

## Verification

1. Run `mkdocs serve` locally to preview
2. Check all internal links work
3. Verify images load correctly
4. Test GitHub Actions deployment
5. Validate navigation (< 3 clicks to any content)

---

## Writing Guidelines

- No LLM bloat: Direct, technical writing
- Lead with visuals: Diagram first, then explanation
- Max 1 scroll per section: Keep pages scannable
- Code examples: Real, working examples only
- Cross-references: Link related content, don't duplicate

Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

5. No clear entry points for different user personas

### TaskUpdate - 2026-02-01 17:12:03 UTC [18:12:03 CEST]

**User Request:** Implement the following plan:

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

## Proposed MkDocs Structure

**Top-level directories in `docs-content/`:**

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `index.md` | Landing page with quick links |
| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |
| `core-systems/` | LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories |
| `architecture/` | System design, health monitoring, data flow |
| `integrations/` | All MCP servers and tools |
| `reference/` | Commands, API, troubleshooting |
| `images/` | Curated images organized by topic |
| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

**Navigation (5 tabs):**
1. **Home** - Quick start, what is coding
2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

---

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation
**Decision: Pull into MkDocs** (user confirmed)
- Consolidate key integration docs into main MkDocs site
- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

---

**User Request:** Implement the following plan:

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

## Proposed MkDocs Structure

**Top-level directories in `docs-content/`:**

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `index.md` | Landing page with quick links |
| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |
| `core-systems/` | LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories |
| `architecture/` | System design, health monitoring, data flow |
| `integrations/` | All MCP servers and tools |
| `reference/` | Commands, API, troubleshooting |
| `images/` | Curated images organized by topic |
| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

**Navigation (5 tabs):**
1. **Home** - Quick start, what is coding
2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

---

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation
**Decision: Pull into MkDocs** (user confirmed)
- Consolidate key integration docs into main MkDocs site
- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

---

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

## Proposed MkDocs Structure

**Top-level directories in `docs-content/`:**

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `index.md` | Landing page with quick links |
| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |
| `core-systems/` | LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories |
| `architecture/` | System design, health monitoring, data flow |
| `integrations/` | All MCP servers and tools |
| `reference/` | Commands, API, troubleshooting |
| `images/` | Curated images organized by topic |
| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

**Navigation (5 tabs):**
1. **Home** - Quick start, what is coding
2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

---

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation
**Decision: Pull into MkDocs** (user confirmed)
- Consolidate key integration docs into main MkDocs site
- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

---

## Files to Create

**MkDocs config:** `mkdocs.yml`

**Getting Started section:**
- `docs-content/getting-started/index.md`
- `docs-content/getting-started/configuration.md`
- `docs-content/getting-started/docker-mode.md`

**Core Systems section:**
- `docs-content/core-systems/index.md`
- `docs-content/core-systems/lsl.md`
- `docs-content/core-systems/ukb-vkb.md`
- `docs-content/core-systems/constraints.md`
- `docs-content/core-systems/trajectories.md`

**Architecture section:**
- `docs-content/architecture/index.md`
- `docs-content/architecture/health-monitoring.md`
- `docs-content/architecture/data-flow.md`

**Integrations section:**
- `docs-content/integrations/index.md`
- `docs-content/integrations/semantic-analysis.md`
- `docs-content/integrations/constraint-monitor.md`
- `docs-content/integrations/browser-access.md`
- `docs-content/integrations/code-graph-rag.md`
- `docs-content/integrations/serena.md`
- `docs-content/integrations/dashboard.md`

**Reference section:**
- `docs-content/reference/index.md`
- `docs-content/reference/commands.md`
- `docs-content/reference/api.md`
- `docs-content/reference/troubleshooting.md`

**Supporting files:**
- `docs-content/stylesheets/extra.css`
- `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`

---

## Key Diagrams to Keep (~30 estimated)

**Architecture:** coding-system-architecture.png, complete-system-overview.png, integration-architecture.png, knowledge-management-architecture.png

**Workflows:** coding-workflow-with-ai.png, knowledge-capture-flow.png, health-verification-flow.png, constraint-violation-handling.png

**Components:** lsl-architecture.png, semantic-analysis-system-overview.png, constraint-monitor-components.png, statusline-architecture.png

**Screenshots:** Health dashboard, VKB visualization

---

## Verification

1. Run `mkdocs serve` locally to preview
2. Check all internal links work
3. Verify images load correctly
4. Test GitHub Actions deployment
5. Validate navigation (< 3 clicks to any content)

---

## Writing Guidelines

- No LLM bloat: Direct, technical writing
- Lead with visuals: Diagram first, then explanation
- Max 1 scroll per section: Keep pages scannable
- Code examples: Real, working examples only
- Cross-references: Link related content, don't duplicate

4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation
**Decision: Pull into MkDocs** (user confirmed)
- Consolidate key integration docs into main MkDocs site
- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

### Write - 2026-02-01 17:12:03 UTC [18:12:03 CEST]

**User Request:** Implement the following plan:

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

## Proposed MkDocs Structure

**Top-level directories in `docs-content/`:**

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `index.md` | Landing page with quick links |
| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |
| `core-systems/` | LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories |
| `architecture/` | System design, health monitoring, data flow |
| `integrations/` | All MCP servers and tools |
| `reference/` | Commands, API, troubleshooting |
| `images/` | Curated images organized by topic |
| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

**Navigation (5 tabs):**
1. **Home** - Quick start, what is coding
2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

---

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation
**Decision: Pull into MkDocs** (user confirmed)
- Consolidate key integration docs into main MkDocs site
- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

---

{
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml",
  "content": "name: Deploy Documentation\n\non:\n  push:\n    branches:\n      - main\n    paths:\n      - 'docs-content/**'\n      - 'mkdocs.yml'\n      - '.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml'\n  workflow_dispatch:\n\npermissions:\n  contents: read\n  pages: write\n  id-token: write\n\nconcurrency:\n  group: \"pages\"\n  cancel-in-progress: false\n\njobs:\n  build:\n    runs-on: ubuntu-latest\n    steps:\n      - uses: actions/checkout@v4\n        with:\n          fetch-depth: 0\n\n      - name: Setup Python\n        uses: actions/setup-python@v5\n        with:\n          python-version: '3.x'\n\n      - name: Cache pip dependencies\n        uses: actions/cache@v4\n        with:\n          path: ~/.cache/pip\n          key: ${{ runner.os }}-pip-${{ hashFiles('requirements-docs.txt') }}\n          restore-keys: |\n            ${{ runner.os }}-pip-\n\n      - name: Install dependencies\n        run: |\n          pip install mkdocs-material mkdocs-minify-plugin\n\n      - name: Build documentation\n        run: mkdocs build --strict\n\n      - name: Upload artifact\n        uses: actions/upload-pages-artifact@v3\n        with:\n          path: ./site\n\n  deploy:\n    environment:\n      name: github-pages\n      url: ${{ steps.deployment.outputs.page_url }}\n    runs-on: ubuntu-latest\n    needs: build\n    steps:\n      - name: Deploy to GitHub Pages\n        id: deployment\n        uses: actions/deploy-pages@v4\n"
}
```

### TaskUpdate - 2026-02-01 17:12:03 UTC [18:12:03 CEST]

**User Request:** Implement the following plan:

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

## Proposed MkDocs Structure

**Top-level directories in `docs-content/`:**

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `index.md` | Landing page with quick links |
| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |
| `core-systems/` | LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories |
| `architecture/` | System design, health monitoring, data flow |
| `integrations/` | All MCP servers and tools |
| `reference/` | Commands, API, troubleshooting |
| `images/` | Curated images organized by topic |
| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

**Navigation (5 tabs):**
1. **Home** - Quick start, what is coding
2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

---

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation
**Decision: Pull into MkDocs** (user confirmed)
- Consolidate key integration docs into main MkDocs site
- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

---

## Files to Create

  "content": "# Getting Started\n\nComplete guide to installing and configuring the coding infrastructure.\n\n## Prerequisites\n\n- **Node.js 18+**\n- **Git**\n- **jq** (JSON processor)\n- **Docker** (optional, for containerized deployment)\n\n=== \"macOS\"\n\n    ```bash\n    brew install git node jq\n    ```\n\n=== \"Linux (Ubuntu/Debian)\"\n\n    ```bash\n    sudo apt update && sudo apt install git nodejs npm jq\n    ```\n\n=== \"Windows\"\n\n    Install via package managers or direct downloads from:\n\n    - [nodejs.org](https://nodejs.org)\n    - [git-scm.com](https://git-scm.com)\n    - [stedolan.github.io/jq](https://stedolan.github.io/jq/)\n\n## Installation\n\n```bash\n# Clone with submodules\ngit clone --recurse-submodules <repository-url> ~/Agentic/coding\ncd ~/Agentic/coding\n\n# Run installer\n./install.sh\n\n# Reload shell\nsource ~/.bashrc  # or ~/.zshrc\n```\n\n### What Gets Installed\n\n| Component | Description |\n|-----------|-------------|\n| `coding` | Launch Claude Code with all integrations |\n| `vkb` | View Knowledge Base (web visualization) |\n| MCP Servers | Semantic Analysis, Constraint Monitor, Browser Access |\n| LSL | Live Session Logging with 4-layer monitoring |\n| Hooks | PreToolUse (constraints) and PostToolUse (logging) |\n\n### Installation Safety\n\nThe installer follows a **non-intrusive policy**:\n\n- Prompts before any system-level changes\n- Creates timestamped backups of shell config\n- Supports `skip-all` to decline all system changes\n\n## Verification\n\n```bash\n# Run test suite (check-only by default)\n./scripts/test-coding.sh\n\n# Interactive repair mode\n./scripts/test-coding.sh --interactive\n\n# Manual verification\nvkb --version\ncoding --help\n```\n\n## First Usage\n\n```bash\n# Launch Claude Code with all systems\ncoding --claude\n\n# Or specify project\ncoding --project ~/my-project\n\n# View knowledge graph\nvkb  # Opens browser to http://localhost:8080\n```\n\n### Knowledge Base Updates\n\nWithin a Claude Code session:\n\n```\n# Incremental analysis (recent changes)\n\"ukb\" or \"update knowledge base\"\n\n# Full analysis (entire codebase)\n\"full ukb\" or \"fully update knowledge base\"\n```\n\n## Next Steps\n\n- [Configuration](configuration.md) - API keys and port setup\n- [Docker Mode](docker-mode.md) - Containerized deployment\n- [Core Systems](../core-systems/index.md) - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints\n"
}

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

## Proposed MkDocs Structure

**Top-level directories in `docs-content/`:**

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `index.md` | Landing page with quick links |
| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |
| `core-systems/` | LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories |
| `architecture/` | System design, health monitoring, data flow |
| `integrations/` | All MCP servers and tools |
| `reference/` | Commands, API, troubleshooting |
| `images/` | Curated images organized by topic |
| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

**Navigation (5 tabs):**
1. **Home** - Quick start, what is coding
2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

---

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation

- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

Services start automatically\n```\n\n### Disable Docker Mode\n\n```bash\nrm .docker-mode\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml down\ncoding --claude  # Now runs in native mode\n```\n\n## Common Operations\n\n```bash\n# View logs\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml logs -f coding-services\n\n# Restart services\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml restart\n\n# Rebuild after code changes\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml build --no-cache\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml up -d\n\n# Full stop\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml down\n\n# Stop and remove volumes (data loss!)\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml down -v\n```\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Container Won't Start\n\n```bash\n# Check logs\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml logs coding-services\n\n# Force rebuild\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml build --no-cache\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml up -d\n```\n\n### Port Conflicts\n\n```bash\n# Find process using port\nlsof -i :3848\n\n# Kill conflicting process or change ports in .env.ports\n```\n\n### Connection Refused\n\n```bash\n# Verify Docker mode is active\nls -la .docker-mode\n\n# Check container status\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml ps\n\n# Test health endpoint\ncurl -v http://localhost:3848/health\n```\n\n### Volume Permission Issues\n\n```bash\n# Fix directory permissions\nmkdir -p .data/knowledge-graph .specstory/history\nchmod -R 755 .data/ .specstory/\n\n# Restart\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml restart\n```\n"

Launches Claude with Docker MCP config\n\n!!! tip \"Alternative\"\n    Set environment variable instead of marker file:\n    ```bash\n    export CODING_DOCKER_MODE=true\n    ```\n\n## Verify Health\n\n```bash\n# Container status\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml ps\n\n# Health endpoints\ncurl http://localhost:3848/health  # Semantic Analysis\ncurl http://localhost:3847/health  # Browser Access\ncurl http://localhost:3849/health  # Constraint Monitor\ncurl http://localhost:3850/health  # Code Graph RAG\n```\n\n## Port Mapping\n\n| Port | Service | Protocol |\n|------|---------|----------|\n| 3847 | Browser Access SSE | HTTP/SSE |\n| 3848 | Semantic Analysis SSE | HTTP/SSE |\n| 3849 | Constraint Monitor SSE | HTTP/SSE |\n| 3850 | Code Graph RAG SSE | HTTP/SSE |\n| 8080 | VKB Server | HTTP |\n| 6333 | Qdrant | HTTP |\n| 6334 | Qdrant | gRPC |\n| 6379 | Redis | TCP |\n| 7687 | Memgraph | Bolt |\n| 3100 | Memgraph Lab | HTTP |\n\n## Architecture\n\nThe Docker architecture consists of:\n\n- **Host Machine**: Claude CLI with lightweight stdio proxies\n- **Container**: MCP SSE servers (semantic-analysis, browser-access, constraint-monitor, code-graph-rag)\n- **Databases**: Qdrant, Redis, Memgraph running in containers\n\nSee [Architecture > Data Flow](../architecture/data-flow.md) for detailed diagrams.\n\n## Switch Between Modes\n\n### Enable Docker Mode\n\n```bash\ntouch .docker-mode\ncoding --claude  # Services start automatically\n```\n\n### Disable Docker Mode\n\n```bash\nrm .docker-mode\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml down\ncoding --claude  # Now runs in native mode\n```\n\n## Common Operations\n\n```bash\n# View logs\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml logs -f coding-services\n\n# Restart services\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml restart\n\n# Rebuild after code changes\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml build --no-cache\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml up -d\n\n# Full stop\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml down\n\n# Stop and remove volumes (data loss!)\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml down -v\n```\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Container Won't Start\n\n```bash\n# Check logs\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml logs coding-services\n\n# Force rebuild\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml build --no-cache\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml up -d\n```\n\n### Port Conflicts\n\n```bash\n# Find process using port\nlsof -i :3848\n\n# Kill conflicting process or change ports in .env.ports\n```\n\n### Connection Refused\n\n```bash\n# Verify Docker mode is active\nls -la .docker-mode\n\n# Check container status\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml ps\n\n# Test health endpoint\ncurl -v http://localhost:3848/health\n```\n\n### Volume Permission Issues\n\n```bash\n# Fix directory permissions\nmkdir -p .data/knowledge-graph .specstory/history\nchmod -R 755 .data/ .specstory/\n\n# Restart\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml restart\n```\n"
}
```

**Result:** ‚úÖ Success
**Output:** ```
File created successfully at: /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/docs-content/getting-started/docker-mode.md
```

**User Request:** Implement the following plan:

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

## Proposed MkDocs Structure

**Top-level directories in `docs-content/`:**

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `index.md` | Landing page with quick links |
| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |
| `core-systems/` | LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories |
| `architecture/` | System design, health monitoring, data flow |
| `integrations/` | All MCP servers and tools |
| `reference/` | Commands, API, troubleshooting |
| `images/` | Curated images organized by topic |
| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

**Navigation (5 tabs):**
1. **Home** - Quick start, what is coding
2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

---

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation
**Decision: Pull into MkDocs** (user confirmed)
- Consolidate key integration docs into main MkDocs site
- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

---

Opens http://localhost:8080\n```\n\n### Constraints\n\n20 active constraints enforce code <USER_ID_REDACTED> via PreToolUse hooks.\n\n```bash\n# View dashboard\nopen http://localhost:3030\n\n# Check compliance\ncurl http://localhost:3031/api/compliance/coding\n```\n\n### Trajectories\n\nReal-time development state displayed in status line.\n\n| State | Icon | Meaning |\n|-------|------|---------|\n| Exploring | EX | Information gathering |\n| On Track | ON | Productive progression |\n| Off Track | OFF | Deviating from path |\n| Implementing | IMP | Active code modification |\n| Verifying | VER | Testing and validation |\n| Blocked | BLK | Intervention preventing action |\n"

**User Request:** Implement the following plan:

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

## Proposed MkDocs Structure

**Top-level directories in `docs-content/`:**

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `index.md` | Landing page with quick links |
| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |
| `core-systems/` | LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories |
| `architecture/` | System design, health monitoring, data flow |
| `integrations/` | All MCP servers and tools |
| `reference/` | Commands, API, troubleshooting |
| `images/` | Curated images organized by topic |
| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

**Navigation (5 tabs):**
1. **Home** - Quick start, what is coding
2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

---

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation
**Decision: Pull into MkDocs** (user confirmed)
- Consolidate key integration docs into main MkDocs site
- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

---

Curated insights, team sharing |\n| **Continuous Learning** | Automatic | Real-time session learning |\n| **VKB** (Visualize) | `vkb` command | Web-based visualization |\n\n!!! note \"Not Parallel retrieval\n\n## UKB (Manual/Batch)\n\n### What It Does\n\n- Analyzes git commits for patterns\n- Interactive structured capture\n- Ontology classification (4-layer pipeline)\n- Git-tracked JSON exports for team sharing\n\n### Usage (Within Claude Code)\n\n```\n# Incremental analysis (recent changes)\n\"ukb\"\n\n# Full analysis (entire codebase)\n\"full ukb\"\n```\n\n### entity classes:\n\n| Class | Description |\n|-------|-------------|\n| ImplementationPattern | Code patterns and best practices |\n| ArchitecturalDecision | System design choices |\n| TechnicalSolution | Problem-solving approaches |\n| WorkflowPattern | Development process patterns |\n| ConfigurationPattern | Setup and configuration knowledge |\n\n## Continuous Learning (Automatic)\n\n### What It Does\n\n- Real-time extraction from LSL exchanges\n- Embedding generation (384-dim or 1536-dim)\n- Semantic search across sessions\n- Budget-aware LLM usage ($8.33/month limit)\n\n### Storage\n\n```\nQdrant (Vector Database):\n  knowledge_patterns (1536-dim)\n  knowledge_patterns_small (384-dim)\n  session_memory (384-dim)\n\nSQLite (.cache/knowledge.db):\n  budget_events\n  knowledge_extractions\n  embedding_cache\n```\n\n### Privacy-First\n\n5-layer sensitivity classification routes data:\n\n- Sensitive data goes to local models (free, private)\n- Safe data goes to remote models (fast, accurate)\n\n## VKB (Visualization)\n\n```bash\n# Start visualization server\nvkb\n\n# Opens browser to http://localhost:8080\n```\n\n### Features\n\n- Interactive force-directed graph\n- Color-coding by entity type\n- Full-text search\n- Filter by type, significance, source\n- Entity relationship exploration\n\n## Comparison\n\n| Aspect | UKB | Continuous Learning |\n|--------|-----|---------------------|\n| Trigger | Manual MCP command | Automatic |\n| Input | Git commits, prompts | LSL exchanges |\n| Storage | GraphDB | Qdrant + SQLite |\n| Collaboration | Git-tracked | Local only |\n| Search | Name/type-based | Semantic similarity |\n\n### When to Use UKB\n\n- Documenting architectural decisions\n- Post-<COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED> knowledge capture\n- Creating team knowledge base\n- Recording bug fix patterns\n\n### When to Use Continuous Learning\n\n- Automatic (always on)\n- Semantic search during development\n- Cross-session continuity\n- Private session learning\n\n## Key Files\n\n**UKB**:\n\n- `lib/knowledge-api/` - Core implementation\n- `.data/knowledge-graph/` - GraphDB storage\n- `.data/knowledge-export/` - JSON exports\n\n**Continuous Learning**:\n\n- `src/live-logging/StreamingKnowledgeExtractor.js`\n- `src/knowledge-management/EmbeddingGenerator.js`\n- `.cache/knowledge.db` - SQLite analytics\n\n**VKB**:\n\n- `bin/vkb` - Start server\n- `integrations/vkb-visualizer/` - Web UI\n"

  "content": "# Constraints - Code <USER_ID_REDACTED> Enforcement\n\nReal-time code <USER_ID_REDACTED> enforcement through PreToolUse hooks.\n\n![Constraint Monitor Components](../images/constraint-monitor-components.png)\n\n## What It Does\n\n- **PreToolUse Hook Enforcement** - Blocks violations BEFORE tool execution\n- **20 Active Constraints** - Security, architecture, code <USER_ID_REDACTED>, PlantUML, documentation\n- **Severity-Based Enforcement** - CRITICAL/ERROR blocks, WARNING/INFO allows\n- **Compliance Scoring** - Real-time 0-10 scoring\n- **Dashboard Monitoring** - Live violation feed at `http://localhost:3030`\n\n## How It Works\n\n![Constraint Violation Handling](../images/constraint-violation-handling.png)\n\n1. **PreToolUse Hook Fires** - Before tool execution\n2. **Constraint Check** - Analyzes parameters against 20 constraints\n3. **Pattern Matching** - Regex patterns detect violations\n4. **Severity Evaluation** - Determines enforcement action\n5. **Decision**:\n   - CRITICAL/ERROR: **BLOCK** (exit code 1)\n   - WARNING/INFO: **ALLOW** with feedback (exit code 0)\n\n## Severity Levels\n\n| Severity | Impact | Enforcement | Tool Call |\n|----------|--------|-------------|-----------|\n| CRITICAL | -3.0 | BLOCK | Prevented |\n| ERROR | -2.0 | BLOCK | Prevented |\n| WARNING | -1.0 | ALLOW | Proceeds with warning |\n| INFO | -0.5 | ALLOW | Proceeds with info |\n\n## Active Constraints\n\n### Security (2) - 100% Detection\n\n| Constraint | Severity |\n|------------|----------|\n| `no-hardcoded-secrets` | CRITICAL |\n| `no-eval-usage` | CRITICAL |\n\n### Architecture (3) - 100% Detection\n\n| Constraint | Severity |\n|------------|----------|\n| `no-parallel-files` | CRITICAL |\n| `debug-not-speculate` | ERROR |\n| `no-evolutionary-names` | ERROR |\n\n### Code <USER_ID_REDACTED> (7)\n\n| Constraint | Severity |\n|------------|----------|\n| `proper-error-handling` | ERROR |\n| `no-console-log` | WARNING |\n| `no-console-error` | WARNING |\n| `no-console-warn` | WARNING |\n| `no-var-declarations` | WARNING |\n| `proper-function-naming` | INFO |\n| `no-magic-numbers` | INFO |\n\n### PlantUML (5)\n\n| Constraint | Severity |\n|------------|----------|\n| `plantuml-standard-styling` | ERROR |\n| `plantuml-file-organization` | INFO |\n| `plantuml-file-location` | WARNING |\n| `plantuml-diagram-workflow` | INFO |\n| `plantuml-readability-guidelines` | INFO |\n\n## Dashboard\n\n**URL**: `http://localhost:3030`\n\n**Features**:\n\n- Real-time violation feed\n- Compliance score gauge (0-10)\n- 7-day trend chart\n- Project selector\n- Constraint toggles\n\n### API Endpoints (Port 3031)\n\n| Endpoint | Method | Description |\n|----------|--------|-------------|\n| `/api/violations` | GET | List violations |\n| `/api/violations` | POST | Log violation |\n| `/api/compliance/:project` | GET | Project compliance score |\n| `/api/constraints` | GET | List enabled constraints |\n| `/api/health` | GET | Health check |\n\n## Configuration\n\n**File**: `integrations/mcp-constraint-monitor/constraints.yaml`\n\n```yaml\n- id: no-hardcoded-secrets\n  group: security\n  pattern: 'API_KEY|SECRET|TOKEN pattern here'\n  message: 'CRITICAL: Potential hardcoded secret detected'\n  severity: critical\n  enabled: true\n  suggestion: Use environment variables instead\n```\n\n### Enable/Disable\n\n```yaml\n- id: no-console-log\n  enabled: false  # Disable this constraint\n```\n\n## Key Files\n\n| File | Purpose |\n|------|---------|\n| `src/hooks/pre-tool-hook-wrapper.js` | PreToolUse hook entry |\n| `src/enforcement/ConstraintEnforcer.js` | Enforcement engine |\n| `constraints.yaml` | Constraint definitions |\n| `src/dashboard/api/` | REST API |\n| `src/dashboard/ui/` | Next.js dashboard |\n\n## Status Line Integration\n\nFormat: `[SHIELD {compliance}% {trajectory}]`\n\nExample: `[SHIELD 94% IMP]` shows 94% compliance and \"implementing\" state.\n"

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`

- 10 integrations with separate docs

4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current

6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|

| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content

**Tool:** Write
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/docs-content/architecture/index.md",
  "content": "# Architecture\n\nSystem design principles and patterns for the coding infrastructure.\n\n![System Architecture](../images/coding-system-architecture.png)\n\n## Key Principles\n\n### 1. Agent-Agnostic Design\n\nThe system supports multiple AI coding assistants through a unified adapter pattern:\n\n![Agent-Agnostic Architecture](../images/agent-agnostic-architecture-components.png)\n\n**Layers**:\n\n1. **Agent Layer** - AI assistants (Claude, CoPilot, future agents)\n2. **Launcher Layer** - Agent-specific startup scripts\n3. **Common Setup Layer** - Shared initialization (`agent-common-setup.sh`)\n4. **Shared Services** - VKB, Semantic Analysis, Constraint Monitor, LSL\n5. **Adapter Layer** - Abstract interface + agent implementations\n\n### 2. Knowledge Persistence\n\nMulti-tier storage for reliability and performance:\n\n**Runtime (Fast)**:\n\n- MCP Memory (Claude)\n- Graphology Graph (in-memory)\n\n**Persistence (Reliable)**:\n\n- LevelDB (persistent graph storage)\n- JSON exports (git-tracked)\n- `.specstory/history/` (session logs)\n\n### 3. Real-Time <USER_ID_REDACTED> Enforcement\n\nPreToolUse hooks intercept tool calls BEFORE execution:\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart LR\n    A[Claude Tool Call] --> B[PreToolUse Hook]\n    B --> C[Constraint Monitor]\n    C -->|Violation| D[BLOCK]\n    C -->|Clean| E[ALLOW]\n    E --> F[Tool Execution]\n```\n\n### 4. 4-Layer Monitoring\n\nProgressive escalation for reliability:\n\n| Layer | Component | Function |\n|-------|-----------|----------|\n| 4 | Service Health | UKB, VKB, Semantic Analysis |\n| 3 | System Verifier | LSL, Constraints, Trajectory |\n| 2 | System Coordinator | Overall health, metrics |\n| 1 | System Watchdog | Critical failures, alerts |\n\n## Deployment Modes\n\n### Native Mode (Default)\n\nMCP servers run as native stdio processes managed by Claude CLI.\n\n- **Pros**: Simple setup, no Docker, lower memory\n- **Cons**: Processes restart with each session\n- **Best for**: Individual developers\n\n### Docker Mode\n\nMCP servers run as HTTP/SSE services in containers.\n\n- **Pros**: Persistent services, shared browser, better isolation\n- **Cons**: Docker required, higher memory\n- **Best for**: Teams, multi-session workflows\n\nSee [Docker Mode](../getting-started/docker-mode.md) for setup details.\n\n## Development Patterns\n\n### Constraint-Based Development\n\nDefine constraints before implementation:\n\n```yaml\nconstraints:\n  - id: no-parallel-versions\n    pattern: /(v\\d+|enhanced|improved|new|fixed)_/\n    severity: CRITICAL\n    message: Never create parallel versions - edit originals\n```\n\n### Agent Detection\n\n```javascript\nconst detector = new AgentDetector();\nconst available = await detector.detectAll();\n// { claude: true, copilot: false }\n\nconst best = await detector.getBest();\n// 'claude'\n```\n\n### Knowledge Capture\n\n```bash\n# Auto-analysis from git commits\nukb\n\n# Structured interactive capture\nukb --interactive\n\n# Visualization\nvkb\n```\n\n## Adding New Agents\n\nSee [Agent Integration Guide](../reference/api.md#agent-integration) for:\n\n1. Implement `AgentAdapter` interface\n2. Register adapter in `agent-registry.js`\n3. Add detection in `agent-detector.js`\n4. Create launcher script\n5. Update `bin/coding` routing\n6. Test with validation commands\n\n## Related Documentation\n\n- [Health Monitoring](health-monitoring.md) - 4-layer architecture details\n- [Data Flow](data-flow.md) - System data flow diagrams\n- [Integrations](../integrations/index.md) - MCP server architectures\n"
}

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

## Proposed MkDocs Structure

**Top-level directories in `docs-content/`:**

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `index.md` | Landing page with quick links |
| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |
| `core-systems/` | LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories |
| `architecture/` | System design, health monitoring, data flow |
| `integrations/` | All MCP servers and tools |
| `reference/` | Commands, API, troubleshooting |
| `images/` | Curated images organized by topic |
| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

**Navigation (5 tabs):**
1. **Home** - Quick start, what is coding
2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

---

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation
**Decision: Pull into MkDocs** (user confirmed)
- Consolidate key integration docs into main MkDocs site
- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

`monitoring/global-monitor-watchdog.js`\n\n**Function**: Top-level supervisor monitoring all monitors\n\n- Restarts failed monitoring processes\n- Logs health status every 60 seconds\n- Acts as last Processing issues\n\n## Layer 4: Service-Level Self-Monitoring\n\n**Component**: Enhanced Transcript Monitor\n\n**Function**: Per-service health reporting\n\n- Generates `.transcript-monitor-health` 7481974,\n    \"uptimeSeconds\": 925,\n    \"processId\": 78406\n  },\n  \"activity\": {\n    \"lastExchange\": \"82da8b2a-6a30-45eb-b0c7-5e1e2b2d54ee\",\n    \"exchangeCount\": 10,\n `/api/services` | GET | Individual service status |\n| `/api/metrics` | GET | Health metrics history |\n| `/api/alerts` | GET | Recent alerts |\n\n## Health Files\n\n| File | Purpose monitoring/transcript-monitor-verifier.js --check\n\n# Restart coordinator\npkill -f global-transcript-monitor-coordinator\nnode monitoring/global-transcript-monitor-coordinator.js &\n\n# Full system restart\n./bin/restart-monitoring.sh\n```\n\n## Alert Thresholds\n\n| Metric | Warning | Critical |\n|--------|---------|----------|\n| Memory Usage | >500MB | >1GB |\n| CPU Usage | >50% | >80% |\n| Stale Monitor | >5 min | >15 min |\n| Processing Delay | >30s | >60s |\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Monitor not updating\n\n```bash\n# Check if process is running\nps aux | grep enhanced-transcript-monitor\n\n# Check health file timestamp\nls -la .health/coding-transcript-monitor-health.json\n\n# Restart monitor\npkill -f enhanced-transcript-monitor\nTRANSCRIPT_SOURCE_PROJECT=\"/path/to/project\" node scripts/enhanced-transcript-monitor.js &\n```\n\n### Coordinator issues\n\n```bash\n# Check coordinator status\ncat .health/coordinator-status.json\n\n# View coordinator logs\ntail -100 .logs/coordinator.log\n\n# Restart coordinator\nnode monitoring/global-transcript-monitor-coordinator.js &\n```\n\n### Health TB\n    subgraph \"User Layer\"\n        U[User] --> CC[Claude Code]\n    end\n\n    subgraph \"Tool Layer\"\n        CC -->|PreToolUse| CM[Constraint Monitor]\n        CM -->|Block/Allow| CC\n        CC -->|Tool Call| MCP[MCP Servers]\n        CC -->|PostToolUse| LSL[LSL Monitor]\n    end\n\n    subgraph \"Analysis Layer\"\n        MCP --> SA[Semantic Analysis]\n        MCP --> BA[Browser Access]\n        MCP --> CGR[Code Graph RAG]\n    end\n\n    subgraph \"Storage Layer\"\n        LSL --> FS[.specstory/history/]\n        SA --> GDB[GraphDB]\n        CGR --> MG[Memgraph]\n        SA --> QD[Qdrant]\n    end\n\n    subgraph \"Visualization\"\n        GDB --> VKB[VKB Server]\n        FS --> VKB\n    end\n```\n\n## LSL Data Flow\n\n![LSL Classification Flow](../images/lsl-classification-flow.png)\n\n**Exchange Processing**:\n\n1. **Capture**: Transcript monitor detects new exchange\n2. **Classify**: 5-layer classifier determines routing\n3. **Redact**: Security patterns sanitized\n4. **Route**: Content written to LOCAL or CODING history\n5. **Log**: Classification decision logged\n\n**Classification Decision Tree**:\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart TD\n    E[Exchange] --> L0{Layer 0: Session Filter}\n    L0 -->|Confident| D[Decision]\n    L0 -->|Uncertain| L1{Layer 1: PathAnalyzer}\n    L1 -->|Confident| D\n    L1 -->|Uncertain| L2{Layer 2: KeywordMatcher}\n    L2 -->|Confident| D\n    L2 -->|Uncertain| L3{Layer 3: EmbeddingClassifier}\n    L3 -->|Confident| D\n    L3 -->|Uncertain| L4{Layer 4: SemanticAnalyzer}\n    L4 --> D\n    D -->|LOCAL| LP[Project History]\n    D -->|CODING| CP[Coding History]\n```\n\n## Knowledge Flow\n\n![Knowledge Capture Flow](../images/knowledge-capture-flow.png)\n\n**UKB Flow**:\n\n1. **Trigger**: MCP command or git analysis\n2. **Extract**: Patterns from commits or prompts\n3. **Classify**: 4-layer ontology pipeline\n4. **Store**: GraphDB (Graphology + LevelDB)\n5. **Export**: JSON for git tracking\n\n**Continuous Learning Flow**:\n\n1. **Monitor**: LSL exchanges captured\n2. **Extract**: StreamingKnowledgeExtractor identifies insights\n3. **Embed**: Generate 384-dim or 1536-dim vectors\n4. **Store**: Qdrant (vectors) + SQLite (metadata)\n5. **Retrieve**: Semantic search available\n\n## Constraint Flow\n\n![Constraint Dataflow](../images/constraint-monitor-dataflow.png)\n\n**PreToolUse Hook Flow**:\n\n1. **Intercept**: Hook fires before tool execution\n2. **Check**: ConstraintEnforcer evaluates parameters\n3. **Match**: PatternMatcher runs regex against 20 constraints\n4. **Score**: ComplianceCalculator updates score\n5. **Decide**: Block (CRITICAL/ERROR) or Allow (WARNING/INFO)\n6. **Log**: Violation logged to dashboard API\n\n## MCP Server Communication\n\n**Native Mode**:\n\n```\nClaude CLI <--stdio--> MCP Server Process\n```\n\n**Docker Mode**:\n\n```\nClaude CLI <--stdio--> Proxy <--HTTP/SSE--> Container Server\n```\n\n## Storage Locations\n\n| System | Storage | Format |\n|--------|---------|--------|\n| LSL | `.specstory/history/` | Markdown |\n| Classification | `.specstory/logs/classification/` | JSONL + MD |\n| Knowledge (UKB) | `.data/knowledge-graph/` | LevelDB |\n| Knowledge Export | `.data/knowledge-export/` | JSON |\n| Continuous Learning | Qdrant + `.cache/knowledge.db` | Vectors + SQLite |\n| Trajectories | `.specstory/trajectory/` | JSON |\n| Health | `.health/` | JSON |\n\n## Cross-System Integration\n\n### LSL + Trajectories\n\nLSL exchanges feed real-time trajectory analysis:\n\n```\nLSL Exchange --> Significance Check --> Trajectory Analyzer --> State Update --> Status Line\n```\n\n### LSL + Knowledge\n\nLSL data feeds both knowledge systems:\n\n```\nLSL Exchange --> StreamingKnowledgeExtractor --> Qdrant\nLSL History --> UKB Git Analysis --> GraphDB\n```\n\n### Constraints + LSL\n\nPostToolUse hooks log all tool interactions:\n\n```\nTool Execution --> PostToolUse Hook --> LSL Logger --> .specstory/history/\n```\n\n### Health + All Systems\n\nHealth monitoring spans all components:\n\n```\nAll Services --> Health Files --> Coordinator --> Dashboard\n```\n"

**User Request:** Implement the following plan:

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

## Proposed MkDocs Structure

**Top-level directories in `docs-content/`:**

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `index.md` | Landing page with quick links |
| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |
| `core-systems/` | LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories |
| `architecture/` | System design, health monitoring, data flow |
| `integrations/` | All MCP servers and tools |
| `reference/` | Commands, API, troubleshooting |
| `images/` | Curated images organized by topic |
| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

**Navigation (5 tabs):**
1. **Home** - Quick start, what is coding
2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

---

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation
**Decision: Pull into MkDocs** (user confirmed)
- Consolidate key integration docs into main MkDocs site
- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

<USER_ID_REDACTED> Assurance\n\nThe QA agent implements feedback loops:\n\n1. **Iteration 1**: Standard parameters, initial <USER_ID_REDACTED> check\n2. **Iteration 2**: Stricter requirements, rejects generic patterns\n3. **Iteration 3**: Maximum threshold, requires concrete evidence\n\n**Entity Evaluation Criteria**:\n\n- Specificity\n- Actionability\n- Evidence\n- Uniqueness\n- Naming\n\n## analysis\nexecute_workflow {\n  \"workflow_name\": \"complete-analysis\"\n}\n\n# Extract patterns\nextract_patterns {\n  \"source\": \"authentication module\",\n  \"pattern_types\": [\"design\", \"security\"]\n}\n```\n\n## Storage\n\n- Entities: `.data/knowledge-graph/` (Graphology + LevelDB)\n- Auto-export: `shared-memory-coding.json` every 30 seconds\n- Insights: **User Request:** Implement the following plan:

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

## Proposed MkDocs Structure

**Top-level directories in `docs-content/`:**

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `index.md` | Landing page with quick links |
| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |
| `core-systems/` | LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories |
| `architecture/` | System design, health monitoring, data flow |
| `integrations/` | All MCP servers and tools |
| `reference/` | Commands, API, troubleshooting |
| `images/` | Curated images organized by topic |
| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

**Navigation (5 tabs):**
1. **Home** - Quick start, what is coding
2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

---

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation
**Decision: Pull into MkDocs** (user confirmed)
- Consolidate key integration docs into main MkDocs site
- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

---

  "content": "# Browser Access\n\nStagehand browser automation via MCP.\n\n## Overview\n\n| Property | Value |\n|----------|-------|\n| Component | `browser-access` |\n| Type | MCP Server |\n| Port (Docker) | 3847 |\n| Framework | Stagehand |\n\n## What It Does\n\nBrowser automation for web interactions, testing, and data extraction.\n\n- **Navigate** - Load URLs in automated browser\n- **Act** - Perform atomic actions (click, type, select)\n- **Extract** - Extract text content from pages\n- **Observe** - Find actionable elements\n- **Screenshot** - Capture page screenshots\n\n## MCP Tools\n\n| Tool | Description |\n|------|-------------|\n| `stagehand_navigate` | Navigate to URL |\n| `stagehand_act` | Perform page actions |\n| `stagehand_extract` | Extract page text |\n| `stagehand_observe` | Find actionable elements |\n| `screenshot` | Capture page screenshot |\n\n## Usage Examples\n\n### Navigate\n\n```\nstagehand_navigate {\n  \"url\": \"https://example.com\"\n}\n```\n\n### Act\n\nActions should be atomic and specific:\n\n```\nstagehand_act {\n  \"action\": \"Click the sign in button\"\n}\n\nstagehand_act {\n  \"action\": \"Type 'hello' into the search input\"\n}\n```\n\n!!! warning \"Atomic Actions\"\n    Avoid compound actions like \"Order me pizza\" or \"Send an email to Paul\".\n    Break them into specific steps.\n\n### Extract\n\n```\nstagehand_extract {}\n```\n\nReturns all text content from current page.\n\n### Observe\n\nUse to find elements for subsequent actions:\n\n```\nstagehand_observe {\n  \"instruction\": \"find the login button\"\n}\n```\n\n### Screenshot\n\n```\nscreenshot {}\n```\n\n## Configuration\n\n**Native Mode**:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"mcpServers\": {\n    \"browser-access\": {\n      \"command\": \"node\",\n      \"args\": [\"/path/to/browser-access/build/index.js\"],\n      \"env\": {\n        \"LOCAL_CDP_URL\": \"ws://localhost:9222\"\n      }\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Docker Mode**:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"mcpServers\": {\n    \"browser-access\": {\n      \"command\": \"node\",\n      \"args\": [\"/path/to/browser-access/dist/stdio-proxy.js\"],\n      \"env\": {\n        \"BROWSER_ACCESS_SSE_URL\": \"http://localhost:3847\"\n      }\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Docker Benefits\n\nIn Docker mode, multiple Claude sessions can share the same browser instance:\n\n- No browser startup overhead per session\n- Persistent browser state\n- Shared tabs and cookies\n- Better resource utilization\n\n## Best Practices\n\n1. **Use observe before act** when unsure about element selectors\n2. **Keep actions atomic** - one action per tool call\n3. **Extract for scraping** - use when you need text, not interactions\n4. **Screenshot sparingly** - prefer observe/extract for data\n\n## Health Check\n\n```bash\n# Docker mode\ncurl http://localhost:3847/health\n```\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Browser not connecting\n\n```bash\n# Check Chrome DevTools Protocol\ncurl http://localhost:9222/json/version\n\n# Verify Docker container\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml logs browser-access\n```\n\n### Actions failing\n\n- Use `stagehand_observe` first to verify element exists\n- Check that action description matches visible text\n- Ensure page has fully loaded before acting\n"
}

**User Request:** Implement the following plan:

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

## Proposed MkDocs Structure

**Top-level directories in `docs-content/`:**

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `index.md` | Landing page with quick links |
| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |
| `core-systems/` | LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories |
| `architecture/` | System design, health monitoring, data flow |
| `integrations/` | All MCP servers and tools |
| `reference/` | Commands, API, troubleshooting |
| `images/` | Curated images organized by topic |
| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

**Navigation (5 tabs):**
1. **Home** - Quick start, what is coding
2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

---

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation
**Decision: Pull into MkDocs** (user confirmed)
- Consolidate key integration docs into main MkDocs site
- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

---
