Never use Serena for editing files.\n    Use standard Edit/Write tools for file modifications.\n\n## Usage\n\n### Search Documentation\n\n```\nsearch_serena_documentation {\n  \"query\": \"authentication flow\"\n}\n```\n\n### Search Code\n\n```\nsearch_serena_code {\n  \"query\": \"UserService\"\n}\n```\n\n### Fetch Documentation\n\n```\nfetch_serena_documentation {}\n```\n\nReturns full documentation from the repository.\n\n## Configuration\n\n```json\n{\n  \"mcpServers\": {\n    \"serena\": {\n      \"command\": \"node\",\n      \"args\": [\"/path/to/serena/build/index.js\"]\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## When to Use\n\n**Use Serena for**:\n\n- Searching for code patterns\n- Understanding unfamiliar code\n- Finding symbol definitions\n- Exploring code structure\n\n**Don't use Serena for**:\n\n- Editing files (use Edit tool)\n- Creating files (use Write tool)\n- Running code (use Bash tool)\n\n## Best Practices\n\n1. **Search before reading** - Use Serena to find relevant files first\n2. **Combine with Read** - After finding files, use Read tool for full content\n3. **Semantic over text** - Prefer semantic search for better results\n\n## Comparison with Code Graph RAG\n\n| Feature | Serena | Code Graph RAG |\n|---------|--------|----------------|\n| AST Analysis | Yes | Yes |\n| Graph Database | No | Yes (Memgraph) |\n| Call Graph | No | Yes |\n| Natural Language | Limited | Full |\n| File Operations | No | Yes |\n| Requires Docker | No | Yes (Memgraph) |\n\nUse Serena for quick searches; use Code Graph RAG for deep analysis.\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Server not starting\n\n```bash\n# Check if Serena is built\nls integrations/serena/build/\n\n# Rebuild if needed\ncd integrations/serena && npm run build\n```\n\n### Search not finding results\n\n- Check that the repository is indexed\n- Try broader search terms\n- Use exact symbol names for precise matches\n"

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `index.md` | Landing page with quick links |
| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |
| `core-systems/` | LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories |
| `architecture/` | System design, health monitoring, data flow |
| `integrations/` | All MCP servers and tools |
| `reference/` | Commands, API, troubleshooting |
| `images/` | Curated images organized by topic |
| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

**Navigation (5 tabs):**
1. **Home** - Quick start, what is coding
2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation
**Decision: Pull into MkDocs** (user confirmed)
- Consolidate key integration docs into main MkDocs site
- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

{
  "file_path": "/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/docs-content/reference/commands.md",
  "content": "# Commands\n\nCLI commands and shell usage reference.\n\n## Core Commands\n\n### coding\n\nLaunch Claude Code with all integrations.\n\n```bash\n# Default launch\ncoding --claude\n\n# Specify project\ncoding --project ~/my-project\n\n# Force specific agent\ncoding --claude    # Claude Code (default)\ncoding --copilot   # GitHub CoPilot\n\n# Docker mode\ntouch .docker-mode && coding --claude\n\n# Help\ncoding --help\n```\n\n### vkb\n\nView Knowledge Base visualization.\n\n```bash\n# Open in browser\nvkb\n\n# Version info\nvkb --version\n\n# Debug mode\nvkb --debug\n```\n\n## Testing Commands\n\n### Installation Test\n\n```bash\n# Check-only mode (default, safe)\n./scripts/test-coding.sh\n\n# Interactive repair\n./scripts/test-coding.sh --interactive\n\n# Auto-repair coding-internal issues\n./scripts/test-coding.sh --auto-repair\n\n# Help\n./scripts/test-coding.sh --help\n```\n\n### LSL Validation\n\n```bash\n# Validate LSL configuration\nnode scripts/validate-lsl-config.js\n\n# Generate repair script\nnode scripts/validate-lsl-config.js --generate-repair\n```\n\n## Docker Commands\n\n### Start/Stop Services\n\n```bash\n# Start all services\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml up -d\n\n# Stop all services\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml down\n\n# Restart\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml restart\n```\n\n### View Logs\n\n```bash\n# All services\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml logs -f\n\n# Specific service\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml logs -f coding-services\n```\n\n### Rebuild\n\n```bash\n# Rebuild after code changes\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml build --no-cache\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml up -d\n\n# Remove volumes (data loss!)\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml down -v\n```\n\n## Health Checks\n\n### Docker Mode\n\n```bash\n# All health endpoints\nfor port in 3847 3848 3849 3850; do\n  echo \"Port $port: $(curl -s http://localhost:$port/health | jq -r '.status')\"\ndone\n```\n\n### Native Mode\n\n```bash\n# LSL monitor health\ncat .health/coding-transcript-monitor-health.json | jq '{status, activity}'\n\n# Container status\ndocker compose -f docker/docker-compose.yml ps\n```\n\n## Knowledge Base\n\n### Within Claude Code Session\n\n```\n# Incremental analysis\n\"ukb\" or \"update knowledge base\"\n\n# Full analysis\n\"full ukb\" or \"fully update knowledge base\"\n```\n\n### Command Line\n\n```bash\n# Purge entities from date\nnode scripts/purge-knowledge-entities.js 2025-12-23\n\n# Dry run\nnode scripts/purge-knowledge-entities.js 2025-12-23 --dry-run\n\n# With options\nnode scripts/purge-knowledge-entities.js 2025-12-23 --team=coding --verbose\n```\n\n## LSL Recovery\n\n```bash\n# Recover LSL files from transcripts\nPROJECT_PATH=/path/to/project CODING_REPO=/path/to/coding \\\n  node scripts/batch-lsl-processor.js from-transcripts ~/.claude/projects/-path-to-project\n\n# Recover specific date range\nPROJECT_PATH=/path/to/project CODING_REPO=/path/to/coding \\\n  node scripts/batch-lsl-processor.js retroactive 2024-12-01 2024-12-03\n```\n\n## Git Submodules\n\n```bash\n# Update all submodules\ngit submodule update --remote\n\n# Initialize missing submodules\ngit submodule update --init --recursive\n\n# Update specific submodule\ngit submodule update --remote integrations/mcp-server-semantic-analysis\n```\n\n## Debugging\n\n### Enable Debug Output\n\n```bash\n# LSL debugging\nDEBUG_STATUS=1 TRANSCRIPT_DEBUG=true node scripts/enhanced-transcript-monitor.js\n\n# Full debug mode\nDEBUG_LSL=1 node scripts/generate-proper-lsl-from-transcripts.js --mode=foreign --verbose\n```\n\n### Process Management\n\n```bash\n# Find running monitors\nps aux | grep enhanced-transcript-monitor\n\n# Kill monitors\npkill -f enhanced-transcript-monitor\n\n# Restart monitoring\ncoding --restart-monitor\n```\n"

### Write - 2026-02-01 17:12:03 UTC [18:12:03 CEST]

**User Request:** Implement the following plan:

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

## Proposed MkDocs Structure

**Top-level directories in `docs-content/`:**

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `index.md` | Landing page with quick links |
| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |
| `core-systems/` | LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories |
| `architecture/` | System design, health monitoring, data flow |
| `integrations/` | All MCP servers and tools |
| `reference/` | Commands, API, troubleshooting |
| `images/` | Curated images organized by topic |
| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

**Navigation (5 tabs):**
1. **Home** - Quick start, what is coding
2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

---

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation
**Decision: Pull into MkDocs** (user confirmed)
- Consolidate key integration docs into main MkDocs site
- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

---

boolean;\n  supportsBrowser(): boolean;\n  supportsHooks(): boolean;\n\n  // Operations\n  initialize(config: AgentConfig): Promise<void>;\n  createMemory(key: string, value: any): Promise<void>;\n  searchMemory(query: string): Promise<Memory[]>;\n  readMemory(key: string): Promise<any>;\n}\n```\n\n### Required APIs for New Agents\n\n| API | Purpose |\n|-----|---------|\n| Transcript generation | JSONL format session logs |\n| Memory operations | create/search/read |\n| Browser automation | navigate/act/extract |\n| Hook support | PreToolUse/PostToolUse |\n\n### Integration Steps\n\n1. Implement `AgentAdapter` interface\n2. Register in `agent-registry.js`\n3. Add detection in `agent-detector.js`\n4. Create launcher script `launch-{agent}.sh`\n5. Update `bin/coding` routing\n6. Test with validation commands\n\n## Webhook Events\n\n### Constraint Violations\n\n```json\n{\n  \"event\": \"constraint.violation\",\n  \"data\": {\n    \"constraintId\": \"no-hardcoded-secrets\",\n    \"severity\": \"critical\",\n    \"project\": \"coding\",\n    \"blocked\": true\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Health Alerts\n\n```json\n{\n  \"event\": \"health.alert\",\n  \"data\": {\n    \"service\": \"lsl\",\n    \"status\": \"degraded\",\n    \"message\": \"High memory usage\"\n  }\n}\n```\n"
}
```

**User Request:** Implement the following plan:

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

## Proposed MkDocs Structure

**Top-level directories in `docs-content/`:**

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `index.md` | Landing page with quick links |
| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |
| `core-systems/` | LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories |
| `architecture/` | System design, health monitoring, data flow |
| `integrations/` | All MCP servers and tools |
| `reference/` | Commands, API, troubleshooting |
| `images/` | Curated images organized by topic |
| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

**Navigation (5 tabs):**
1. **Home** - Quick start, what is coding
2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

---

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation
**Decision: Pull into MkDocs** (user confirmed)
- Consolidate key integration docs into main MkDocs site
- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

---

5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation
**Decision: Pull into MkDocs** (user confirmed)
- Consolidate key integration docs into main MkDocs site
- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

## Proposed MkDocs Structure

**Top-level directories in `docs-content/`:**

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `index.md` | Landing page with quick links |
| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |
| `core-systems/` | LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories |
| `architecture/` | System design, health monitoring, data flow |
| `integrations/` | All MCP servers and tools |
| `reference/` | Commands, API, troubleshooting |
| `images/` | Curated images organized by topic |
| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

1. **Home** - Quick start, what is coding
2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation

- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

**User Request:** Implement the following plan:

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

## Proposed MkDocs Structure

**Top-level directories in `docs-content/`:**

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `index.md` | Landing page with quick links |
| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |
| `core-systems/` | LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories |
| `architecture/` | System design, health monitoring, data flow |
| `integrations/` | All MCP servers and tools |
| `reference/` | Commands, API, troubleshooting |
| `images/` | Curated images organized by topic |
| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

**Navigation (5 tabs):**
1. **Home** - Quick start, what is coding
2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

---

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation
**Decision: Pull into MkDocs** (user confirmed)
- Consolidate key integration docs into main MkDocs site
- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

---

5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

---

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation
**Decision: Pull into MkDocs** (user confirmed)
- Consolidate key integration docs into main MkDocs site
- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

## Proposed MkDocs Structure

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|

| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

## Proposed MkDocs Structure

**Top-level directories in `docs-content/`:**

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `index.md` | Landing page with quick links |
| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |
| `core-systems/` | LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories |
| `architecture/` | System design, health monitoring, data flow |
| `integrations/` | All MCP servers and tools |
| `reference/` | Commands, API, troubleshooting |
| `images/` | Curated images organized by topic |
| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

**Navigation (5 tabs):**
1. **Home** - Quick start, what is coding
2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

---

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation

- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

### Bash - 2026-02-01 17:12:03 UTC [18:12:03 CEST]

**User Request:** Implement the following plan:

# Documentation Restructuring Plan

## Current State Analysis

**Inventory:**
- 57 markdown files in `docs/`
- 153 PNG images in `docs/images/`
- ~100+ PUML source files
- 10 integrations with separate docs
- Total: ~405 documentation assets

**Problems:**
1. Documentation sprawled across multiple locations
2. Redundant content (multiple VSCode docs, repeated architecture explanations)
3. Unorganized images directory (153 PNGs, many outdated)
4. Historical/obsolete content mixed with current
5. No clear entry points for different user personas
6. Integration docs disconnected from main docs

---

## Proposed MkDocs Structure

**Top-level directories in `docs-content/`:**

| Directory | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|
| `index.md` | Landing page with quick links |
| `getting-started/` | Installation, configuration, docker |
| `core-systems/` | LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories |
| `architecture/` | System design, health monitoring, data flow |
| `integrations/` | All MCP servers and tools |
| `reference/` | Commands, API, troubleshooting |
| `images/` | Curated images organized by topic |
| `stylesheets/` | Custom CSS |

**Navigation (5 tabs):**
1. **Home** - Quick start, what is coding
2. **Core Systems** - LSL, UKB/VKB, Constraints, Trajectories
3. **Architecture** - System design, diagrams
4. **Integrations** - All MCP servers and tools
5. **Reference** - Commands, API, troubleshooting

---

## Implementation Steps

### Phase 1: Setup MkDocs Infrastructure
1. Create `mkdocs.yml` in coding root
2. Create `docs-content/` directory structure
3. Create `.github/workflows/deploy-docs.yml`
4. Add `stylesheets/extra.css` for custom branding

### Phase 2: Content Curation
1. Identify essential docs from current 57 markdown files
2. Select key diagrams from 153 PNGs (estimate: keep ~30)
3. Consolidate redundant content (e.g., merge VSCode docs)
4. Write new concise pages where needed

### Phase 3: Image Organization
1. Audit all 153 PNGs - categorize as: Essential, Redundant, Obsolete
2. Move essential images to `docs-content/images/` with clear naming
3. Move obsolete to `docs/_obsolete/images/`

### Phase 4: Archive Obsolete Content
Create `docs/_obsolete/` with old markdown, unused PUML, deprecated screenshots

### Phase 5: Integration Documentation
**Decision: Pull into MkDocs** (user confirmed)
- Consolidate key integration docs into main MkDocs site
- Each integration gets a dedicated page with: Overview, Setup, Usage, Configuration
- Integration READMEs become thin pointers: "Full documentation at [MkDocs site]"
- Source of truth moves to MkDocs, not scattered READMEs

### Phase 6: GitHub Actions
Copy and adapt from ui-template for auto-deployment to GitHub Pages

---

## Files to Create

**Getting Started section:**
